File: Theory D&D\Concepts\Magic\The Elements.md

#Concept #Magic
The elements are the naturally ocurring elements, that are often used in [[Theory D&D/Concepts/Magic/Magic]] due to their simplicity. 

The elements so far are:
- [[Electricity]]
- [[Water]]
- [[Fire]]
- [[Wind]]
- [[Soul]]
- [[Light]]
- Earth 

Now, these are conceptually very simple, and most of them are related to [[Life]] itself, making them essential in learning magic. 

And [[God]] said: "Let there be [[Light]]!" and it was lit. 
Water came second, right after the [[Death]] of [[The God]]. 
Then, a [[Soul]] flowed into every living being. 
As the first sparks of thought appeared in a creatures brain, [[Electricity]] was born. 
And the first embers that lit up a [[Fire]] were the ashes of the first man who died. 

Water is the ichor of god. [[The Earth]] is it's body. This means that the being we know as mother nature was god itself. This does also mean that other planets are gods themselves. Dead or alive, we do not know, perhaps not functioning enough to have will, or too highly functioning for us to comprehend. 

Since we know that [[Fire]] is alive, and is the manifestation of a soul, it would mean that [[The Sun]] is enshrouded in living beings, the same way that [[The Earth]] is. Making them both gods. 
The people naming planets after gods wasn't a coincidence. The planets are gods. 


File: Theory D&D\Theories\Philosophical\The God of the Gaps never Existed.md

#Theory 
# **Explanation:**
Whenever a gap in the human understanding is formed, that is where the christians fill it with a [[God]], and that is where [[The God]]
of the gaps comes from. Whenever humanity says there is a [[God]], that’s because people can’t explain something, and god makes for a good scapegoat.

A lazy writeoff for understanding, Henry said that whenever christians don’t understand something, they fill it with [[God]]. [[God]] has to be [[The God]] of everything, or he simply doesn’t exist. 

In other words, we can’t have god be this spontaneous miracle worker, that shows up to fill things we can’t quite explain, and then fill the rest away as natural processes of science. Either [[God]] is absolute, or [[God]] doesn’t exist. 

This is the reason that the belief in christianity has declined so much in the past century, Before modern science there wasn’t a way to explain the world outside of some supernatural entity. Since then, gaps have gotten smaller, and that has made [[God]] smaller. 

If there is a [[God]], it has to be an absolute [[God]].
# **Interpretation:**
There’s one super [[God]] that exists above all other regular, conceptual gods, that is the embodiment of EVERYTHING. (if there wasn’t there couldn’t be a [[God]], which disproves the existence of all other gods)


File: Theory D&D\Concepts\Entities\Gods\The God.md

#Character #God 
# Things to note:

- Is the embodiment of EVERYTHING. EVERYTHING is ULTIMATE GOD. 
    
- Wrote the laws of the universe, can rewrite the laws of the universe. 
    
- People proficient with [[Pattern Manipulation]] can perceive this entity for what it truly is. They can use this ability to perform acts of [[Theory D&D/Concepts/Magic/Magic]]. 
    
- Inhabits the [[Hyper Reality]].
    
- HE DOESN’T EXIST, as he gave a part of himself to create everything, as everything other than him is imperfect. If you combine everything in the world, you still get him, but has to be everything
- The [[Blood|Ichor]] running through his veins is [[Water]]


counts as a [[God]]

File: Theory D&D\Things\Locations\Structures\The Math Vault of Trinidad.md

#Location 
On the island of Trinidad, off the coast of [[Venezuela]], there is [[The Math Vault of Trinidad]]. Around a series of caves and caverns in the area ([[Hollow Earth]]), there are several mathematical equations carved into rock. Anyone who looks at them, it feels like utter nonsense. 
These numbers are a [[God|Divine]] number, and the reason they look senseless to most [[Human]]s, is because they do not have the ability of [[Pattern Manipulation]], or they haven't achieved [[Enlightenment]] yet. The person who can solve these equations, or who can read them will be able to unlock an entrance into the [[Hollow Earth]]. 

Also allows connection with the aliens, which means that the hollow earth inhabitants are in kahoots with [[Alien]]s.

File: Theory D&D\Theories\Locational\The Ocean at Night.md

#Theory 
[[Vertical Migration]]
In the gulf of Aiden, in 2010, there was a project for something called the [[The Artificial Sun]]. They set a fake sun on the ocean, and that woke up a very large sea [[Cryptid]]. There were 82 [[Earthquake|earthquake]]s recorded around the area in a 48 hour period. After that, 27 different world navies sent their soldiers to fight "[[Pirate|Pirates]]" around the area. Text log leaks show that there was a giant vortex in the area. There is this giant [[Ses-Syquamlich]] that preys on whales and sharks, and that's a big Lovecraftian monster that just lives in [[The Ocean]].

File: Theory D&D\Things\Weapons\The Pequod Specifications.md

#Thing #Document
## Base Platform: Modified _Komsomolets_-Class (Project 685) Derivative

While the Pequod shares its pressure hull architecture with the deep-diving [[Soviet Union|Soviet]] design, it has been extensively modified for autonomous operation and weaponized deployment.

| Specification              | Value                                                                      |
| -------------------------- | -------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| **Displacement**           | 5,900 tons (surfaced) / 7,200 tons (submerged)                             |
| **Length**                 | 117.5 meters                                                               |
| **Beam**                   | 10.2 meters                                                                |
| **Pressure Hull Material** | Titanium alloy (40% thicker than standard, capable of 1,800m crush depth)  |
| **Propulsion**             | 1 × OK-650B pressurized water reactor (modified for silent running)        |
| **Shaft Power**            | 43,000 shp                                                                 |
| **Speed**                  | 12 knots (silent station-keeping) / 38 knots (maximum)                     |
| **Endurance**              | Nuclear: unlimited / Crew provisions: 0 (unmanned)                         |
| **Test Depth**             | 1,400 meters (operational) / 1,700 meters (maximum before hull compromise) |
| **Complement**             | None - fully autonomous                                                    |
## Autonomous Systems

### Command Architecture

- **Primary AI**: "Claude Sonnet 4.5"
- **Backup Systems**: Three independent neural networks running in constant consensus-voting configuration.
- **Communications**: ELF (Extremely Low Frequency) receive-only for mission updates; no active transmissions permitted.
### Sensory Suite

| System                           | Purpose                                                                                                                         |
| -------------------------------- | ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| **Passive Sonar Array**          | Towed array extending 1.8km behind vessel - calibrated specifically for sub-10Hz infrasound generation                          |
| **Seismic Detectors**            | Can register crustal displacement from 0.1 Richter scale                                                                        |
| **Bioluminescence Scanners**     | Optical sensors tuned to 470nm                                                                                                  |
| **Pressure Wave Interferometry** | Detects massive displacement currents at ranges up to 40km                                                                      |
| **Magnetohydrodynamic Sensors**  | The Ses-Syquamlich generates measurable EM fields when moving at depth; these sensors can track it through the seafloor itself. |
## Armament

### Primary Weapon: Modified W-87 Nuclear Warhead

| Parameter           | Specification                                                               |
| ------------------- | --------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| **Yield**           | 475 kilotons (variable yield - can be reduced to 5kt for precision strikes) |
| **Delivery System** | Internal launch tube, horizontal ejection                                   |
| **Warhead Type**    | Enhanced radiation/neutron - optimized for biological targets at depth      |
| **Fusing**          | Proximity (adaptive) / Contact / Timed                                      |
## Mission Profile

**Station:** The Pequod maintains a continuous loiter at 1,200 meters depth, approximately 60km from the last confirmed sighting coordinates. It performs a vertical ascent to 600m every 72 hours to refresh sensor sweeps.

**Engagement Criteria:**

1. Detection of seismic signature matching Ses-Syquamlich emergence (0.8-1.2 Richter, unique waveform)
2. Confirmation via three independent sensor systems
3. Target identification at >80% confidence
4. No surface vessels within 200km (collateral avoidance)

**Firing Solution:** The missile is ejected horizontally, ignites at 300m separation, and climbs to intercept trajectory. Detonation occurs at optimal standoff distance determined by real-time analysis of creature's position and depth.

**Post-Detonation Protocol:** The Pequod will immediately dive to maximum depth and maintain silent running for 30 days, then ascend to verify kill via:
- Absence of seismic signatures
- Tissue samples in water column
- Disruption of deep-sea food chain patterns
## Notable Incidents

- **2010 (Gulf of Aden incident)**: The Pequod tracked the Ses-Syquamlich for 14 hours following the Artificial Sun activation. Firing solution was acquired but overridden by Illuminati High Council when 27 naval vessels entered the area to investigate "piracy." The creature was not seen again for 18 months.
- **2014**: The submarine detected the creature emerging near the Mid-Atlantic Ridge and tracked it for 6 days before losing the trail in a hydrothermal vent field. Analysis suggests the Ses-Syquamlich may have multiple lairs connected through underwater cave systems.
- **2019**: A scheduled maintenance window was delayed by 4 months due to "unusual activity" in the patrol zone. When the support vessel arrived, the Pequod's logs showed it had fired a warning shot (5kt yield) to deter the creature from approaching surface shipping lanes. The Illuminati officially "does not confirm" this event.

File: Theory D&D\Things\Weapons\The Pequod.md

#Thing 
The Pequod is an autonimous submarine owned by the [[Illuminati]], with the single purpose of sending it's [[Nuke|Nuclear Missile]], to kill the [[Ses-Syquamlich]]. It remains perpetually motioned around the lower levels of the [[Bermuda Triangle]], awaiting completion of it's purpose. 

To learn more, see [[The Pequod Specifications]]

#Concept #Religion
The belief that there are Masters in this world, mostly around Tibet, who have gathered great wisdom and supernatural powers. They are trying to revive knowledge of an ancient religion once found around the world that will again come to eclipse existing world religions. 

Also the religion that there is one hidden truth in the world, which if you learn, you can begin manipulating with. And there are some reality hackers who have figured out what the one truth is, which are known as the Masters. They understand how [[The Universe]] works. They can perform [[Theory D&D/Concepts/Magic/Magic]], and witchcraft, because they understand how the world works better than we do.

File: Theory D&D\Theories\Locational\Timecube.md

#Theory 
This is about a website that was made in 1997, by one Jean
It's about [[Time]] not working in a linear line, and there are 4 sides of time that we travel through. 
Because of this, every day 96 hours actually occur, but we only experience 24. The other hours are experienced in their respective timelines. 
At mid day and mid night [[The Sun]] and [[The Moon]] are perfectly in sync, and people cross over from one timeline into another. #[[Ascension]]

So yeah, there are 4 timelines. cool. 
The 4 guardians at the corners of time are:
	[[Jesus]]
	[[Albert Einstein]]
	[[Socrates]]
	[[Bill Clinton]]

File: Theory D&D\Concepts\Science\Timeline Hopping.md

#Concept 
Timeline Hopping is when you jump from one [[Time]]line into another. This usually happens at the corners of time, as explained in [[Timecube]], 

There are two main ways to perform timeline hopping:
- The Doppelganger Method:
	- By using a [[Ritual]], or some sort of [[Theory D&D/Concepts/Magic/Magic]], or interplanar travel, you can jump into another timeline, but this usually results in an [[Angel]] tracking you down, and returning you to your own timeline, but taking your [[Soul]] as punishment for trying to cheat the system. 
- The Swap Method: 
	- By aligning yourself with the other you in the same place, at the same time, you can swap your consciousness with the other individual. This is the more safer option, as this can't be traced by [[Angel]]s. This is incredibly hard to pull of though.

File: Theory D&D\Theories\Locational\Top of Mountains.md

#Theory 
# Explanation

There is a cosmic sort of power or importance to [[Mountain]] tops. If there’s an unseen supernatural or [[Vibrations|vibrational]] world around us, mountains are the peak where they transition from our world into theirs. This is mostly due to the lack of interference of other vibrational forces that are at the lower points on earth. The construction of [[The Pyramids]] was also to simulate the top of a mountain, and be more powerful. 

Since [[Jesus]] ascended on the top of a [[Mountain]], it’s the gateway between this world and the metaphysical.

Some [[Cryptid]]s can use the gateway at the top of the mountains to traverse out of our field of comprehension.

File: Theory D&D\Things\Magic\Primal Spells\Trigger.md

#Spell #Magic #Enchantment #Lisal 
- Description:
	- A rather simple spell, that allows you to cast a second spell upon a specific trigger. 
- Components:
	- Magical:
		- (2) The spell deals 1d4 soul damage to the caster.
	- Ancillary:
		- (3) The components for the target spell must be cast. 
	- Mental: 
		- (1) The caster must think of the word "Gelios"
		- (4) The trigger for the spell must be selected by the caster from the list below:
			- There isn't a word specified within 20 seconds of casting the spell:
				- The spell triggers instantly, whenever it is able to. 
					- Note that this is very dangerous, and should never be done.
			- "Varda"
				- The spell triggers upon a verbal component is fufilled. When the word/phrase is spoken by the caster, the spell will trigger. This adds a verbal component to this spell and increases the magical component by a bit:
					- (5) The chosen phrase must be spoken by the caster. 
					- (2.1) The caster takes 1d6 additional soul damage. 
			- "Darba"
				- The spell triggers upon a somatic component is fufilled. When a movement is performed by the caster, the spell will trigger. This adds a somatic component to this spell and increases the magical component by a bit:
					- (5) The chosen movement must be performed by the caster. 
					- (2.1) The caster takes 1d6 additional soul damage. 
			- "Doma"
				- The spell triggers upon a mental component is fufilled. When the word/phrase/concept is thought of by the caster, the spell will trigger. This adds a mental component to this spell and increases the magical component by a bit:
					- (5) The chosen word/phrase/concept must be thought of by the caster. 
					- (2.1) The caster takes 3d6 additional soul damage. 
			- "Und"
				- The spell gains an additional trigger that must be fufilled in order for the spell to be cast. This functions as a logical AND gate.
					- This increases the Magical component by 1 soul damage
			- "Esto"
				- The spell gains an additional trigger that can be completed instead of the current trigger in order for the spell to be cast. This functions as a logical OR gate.
					- This increases the Magical component by 1 soul damage
			- "Rotos"
				- The spell will NOT be completed if the following trigger is active. Functions as a logical NOT gate. 
- Variations:
	- By casting the spell two times on the same target spell, the target spell will be triggered four times.
	- By casting the spell three times on the same target spell, the target spell will trigger infinitely, until dispelled, or until the trigger spell runs out of ambient [[Mana]] to cast the spell, and breaking this spell in the process. 
	- The ambient mana to trigger a spell will be sourced from the casters reserves. If the caster is at least 100 ft away from the trigger location of the spell, the spell will not affect 
- Limitations:
	- If there is insufficient ambient mana, the target spell won't be recast again, and the trigger spell will end. 

File: Theory D&D\Things\Other\UFO.md

#Thing 
An UFO is an unidentified flying object. Often connected with [[Alien]].
There are three types of UFO's:
-  Nano-UFO: Small enough to enter a [[Human]]'s bloodstream, and turn them into a [[Sleeper Agent]]. 
- Giga-UFO: Large enough to be clouds, [[Star]]s, or the entire [[Sky]] itself. These mostly exist for [[Surveilance System|surveilance]] reasons, because we exist in [[The Simulation|A Simulation]].

File: Theory D&D\Theories\Locational\Underground Caverns.md

#Theory 
This is of course related to [[Hollow Earth]]. 
The tibetan holy books said that beneath mount everest there were these tunnel systems that spread all over the world. 
The majority of cave systems are completely unexplored. 

Most of these systems are closed up by [[The Government]], and in most cases it is a felony if you try to access them. This means that the government doesn't want us to get into the [[Hollow Earth]]. because obviously.

Also every single culture has a legend of creatures that come from underground. Also religions having the common idea of [[Demon]]s living underneath, and troglodytes living underground as well, and the idea that you can dig your way down into [[Hell]] (which of course is a psyops, because beneath us is [[Heaven]], obviously.) 
Underneath [[The Pyramids]] there is a massive underground cave system, and the structures in [[Antartica]] were a signal to get underground. Also some ancient societies just disappearing into caves all at once.

File: Theory D&D\Theories\Philosophical\Upward Causality.md

#Theory 
Cause and effect, but backwards.

The animal that wants to eat another animal makes that other animal have the desire to eat food, which makes the food to have the desire to take in water, which makes the sky want to produce more water.

This is related to [[The Simulation]] theory. If you, as the person, need to intake food, the system puts more food into it, so it has to supply water for the food and etc, and etc. So we are beings that make the food appear, instead of the food being there is what lets us be alive. 

File: Theory D&D\Theories\Souls n shit\Vaccine Soul Stealing.md


In the early 2000s, [[The CIA]] got into gene editing. The CIA was interested into something known as the fundamentalist gene. The idea is that it's a gene that allows people to have a belief or calling to a higher power. The CIA wanted to know if there was a way to chemically castrate this. They created [[Vaccine]]s that were carried out overseas, so that people can lose faith in [[God]], and lose their [[Soul]]. This is so the highest authority is [[The Government]] of the [[United States]]. This is vaguely related to the [[Hydrophobia Experiments]] going on in around the same time. 

File: Theory D&D\Things\Medicine\Vaccine.md

#Thing #Medicine

File: Theory D&D\Theories\Useless\Valley of Lost Candles.md

#Theory 
Is in reference to stolen props from the 1967 movie "Valley Of The Dolls."
Because of the shady stuff that happens in holywood, the film was seen as a look behind the scenes of what happens in there. 
Several of the props like the candles used in the movie were used in actual [[Theory D&D/Concepts/Magic/Magic|witchcraft]] [[ritual]]s, and carried bad spirits with them. Those props were stolen immediately after the movie.

File: Theory D&D\Concepts\Science\Vertical Migration.md

#Concept 
If there is a creature that does not like the light, and prefers the darkness, then as [[The Sun]] goes up, it goes deeper under[[Water|water]], and as the sun goes down, it goes closer to the surface. 

File: Theory D&D\Theories\Locational\Space\Vertical Universe.md

#Theory 
We are moving in a directly straight line through [[The Universe]], with the existence above us and below us being somewhere we can't really reach. [[God]]s are beings that are capable of moving to different times, by using [[Time Travel]].

File: Theory D&D\Concepts\Science\The Natural Forces\Vibrations.md

#Concept 
A vibration is when particles oscillate at a rate exceeding 1 Hz. 

[[Masaru Emoto]] proved that vibrations in [[The Earth]], and in the [[Wind]] can heal a [[Human]] [[Body]]. This was later expanded upon by [[Esero Khuga]], who achieved partial [[Immortallity]] with a technique based on this basis. 

File: Theory D&D\Things\Magic\Misc\Virus 23.md

#Magic #Thing #Entity
[[Theory D&D/Theories/Spiritual/Virus 23|Virus 23]]

**# Things to note:

- Can be hidden into anything. 
    
- When you observe a material with virus 23 in it, you get virus 23, which means that you get depression, sadness, and perhaps a part of your [[Soul]] is sucked out, and you become [[Soulless]]
    

- When your soul is sucked out, it means that it has to go somewhere, so I guess the virus feeds on souls that it sucks from people? Except it doesn’t really grow stronger, so perhaps the souls actually can be harvested from the virus. This explains ambient [[Mana]], and ambient energy. 
    

- This is one of the sources from which ambient mana comes into the world. 
    
- A mutated, more developed version exists as the absolute [[Hyper Beast]] in the [[Hyper Reality]], that can’t be brought down by [[Theory D&D/Things/Magic/Misc/Depression Overriding|Depression Overriding]]. This beast gives you the ultimate [[Depression]], and causes you to commit [[Suicide]] in the end.
This is a [[Memetic Hazard]].

File: Theory D&D\Theories\Locational\Volcanoes Real Purpose.md

#Theory 
[[Volcano|Volcanoes]] are an amalgamation of [[Heat|Thermal]] and [[Nuclear]] Energy. The Nuclear Power plants from [[The Great Cycle|the previous cycle]] are the volcanic rocks beneath us, that become the volcanoes that we stand upon.  The volcanoes are some of the last remaining remnants of this old world. 

File: Theory D&D\Theories\Political\War is fake.md

#Theory 
There were never any motivations for [[War]]s.
The motivations for wars were never about money or land, or whatever, but instead more important ideas, such as [[Hydrophobia Experiments]]. 
That does mean that some of the wars were started by [[Illuminati]]. 

File: Theory D&D\Theories\Proven by Other Theories already\Water is not from Earth.md

#Theory 
[[Water]] is naturally acidic, and can do things like erosion. 
With the water cycle on earth, there doesn't seem to be a process that jumpstarted this. 
Water came from an outside source (the core of [[The Earth]], duh)
But yeah, we already proved this theory

File: Theory D&D\Things\Materials\Water.md

#Thing #Material #God #Magic 
# Things to note:

- Water is alive, because water is a part of [[The God]], the same way a [[Human]] with their [[Soul]] is.
    
- Water is the ichor coming from the veins of [[The God]]. That’s why every creature with enough water in them has the ability of choice, and free will. 
    
- Water is capable of growing differently based on environments it remains in, and it changes depending on how the people around it function. 
    
- Water can accumulate positive or [[Negative Energy]] around it. 
- Water is one of [[The Elements]]. 
- Water can be used to put out [[Omega Fire]]

# Related Theories:

- [[Dr Emoto's Water Experiments]]
    

File: Theory D&D\Theories\Locational\Space\Welteislehre.md

#Theory 
World of ice, also known as glacial cosmogony. 
It was an idea brought forward by some dude about the existence of humanity. He was looking at the moon and thought that the irridesence of it is exactly like that of [[Water|ice]]. Then he was  shown a dream where Ice broke apart and made everything as we know it. He came to the idea that the base root of everything in [[The Universe]] was ice. This is close, but this only is true for all the beings on [[The Earth]]. 

This is researched by the germans in the WWII. 


File: Theory D&D\Things\Medicine\Diseases\Wetiko.md

#Thing #Disease
A native [[United States|American]] legend, that has to do with the spirit of greed and selfishness.
It is a virus that people can get infected with, that makes you think of yourself, instead of a community. 
The root word for Wetiko is the same as the root word for [[Wendigo]], but instead of one becoming [[Cannibal|cannibalistic]], and [[Gluttony]] overtaking one, the desire for [[Pride]] and [[Greed]] overtakes them. 
This disease of the Wetiko has affected entire countries or the world at this point. The world looks less at the progression of the world, and more at the progression of self. 

Somehow related to [[Soy]] too if you think about it. 



File: Theory D&D\Theories\Locational\Space\World Wraps.md

#Theory 
# Explanation
The way pacman goes off and back on the opposite sides of the screen, that is how the universe works. The idea is that if you travel far enough in one direction, you’ll wrap back to where you started, and we are contained within this infinite loop. The universe is infinite because of this. This is a way to keep us in the simulation.

# Interpretation
eh, just a random extra rule on how the universe works, not much to do here, due to the incomprehensible distance between us, and the edge of the universe.

[[The Universe]]

File: Theory D&D\Concepts\Entities\Cryptids\Zombie.md

#Entity #Cryptid #Concept 
A [[Zombie]] is a creature, most usually a [[Human]], that has the ability to spread it's condition of being a [[Zombie]] to other creatures, most usually humans. 

Most of the zombies are agressive, and will try to convert as many people to their side as they are capable of.
